***ледниковый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ледниковый.html>ледниковый</a> (25515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ледник.html>ледни́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ledník</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ледниковый.html>леднико́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lednikóvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> glacier; glacial
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ледниковый.html>леднико́вое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:озеро.html>о́зеро</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lednikóvoje</b> ózero</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>glacial</b> lake</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ледниковый.html>леднико́вое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>по́ле</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lednikóvoje</b> póle</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ice field</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>glacier</b> field</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лед.html>лёд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ice
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ледовый.html>ледо́вая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обстановка.html>обстано́вка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ledóvaja</b> obstanóvka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>ice</b> conditions</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ледовый.html>ледо́вая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разведка.html>разве́дка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ledóvaja</b> razvédka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>ice</b> patrol</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ледовый.html>ледо́вые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плавание.html>пла́вания</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ledóvyje</b> plávanija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Arctic voyages</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>ice</b> voyages</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9B%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%BE%D0%B5_%D0%BF%D0%BE%D0%B1%D0%BE%D0%B8%D1%89%D0%B5" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ru:Ледовое побоище"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ледовый.html>ледо́вое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:побоище.html>побо́ище</a></a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ledóvoje</b> pobóišče</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_on_the_Ice" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Battle on the Ice">Battle on the <b>Ice</b></a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">defeat of Germans by Novgorodians in 1242</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***лежавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лежавший.html>лежа́вший</a> (216)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежавший.html>лежа́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ležávšij</span>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ležátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***лежанка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лежанка.html>лежа́нка</a> (15900)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ležátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́нка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежанка.html>лежа́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ležánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежанка.html>лежа́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежанка.html>лежа́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежанка.html>лежа́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sleeping ledge above a Russian chimney stove</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sleeping place or couch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> niche in the stone wall of a crypt, where the deceased is placed</li></ol>

***лежать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́ть</a> (216)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ležati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*legʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ležátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полежать.html>полежа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lie <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to be in a horizontal position</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчик</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:излечение.html>излече́нии</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Málʹčik <b>ležál</b> na izlečénii.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A boy lay in recovery.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be situated</li>
<li>to rest, to be incumbent</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лежачий.html>лежа́чий</a> (14364)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ležátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-áčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежачий.html>лежа́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ležáčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lying, recumbent
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лежачий.html>лежа́чий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ležáčij</b> bolʹnój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">bed patient; cot case</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лежачий.html>лежа́чее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ležáčeje</b> položénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reclining position</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лежачий.html>лежа́чий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>ка́мень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>вода́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:течь.html>течёт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pod ležáčij kámenʹ vodá ne tečót</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> no pains, no gains</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежачий.html>лежа́чего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бью́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ležáčevo ne bʹjut</i> ― <span class="e-translation">never hit a man when he is down</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лежачий.html>лежа́чего</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne bej ležáčevo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> easy as a pie; a piece of cake</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лежачий.html>лежа́чего</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rabóta - ne bej ležáčevo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a no-sweat job</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежачий.html>лежа́чий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полицейский.html>полице́йский</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ležáčij policéjskij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sleeping policeman; speed bump</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>sleeping
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лежачий.html>лежа́чие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вагон.html>ваго́не</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ležáčije</b> mesta v vagóne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(sleeping) berths</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ležátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бище</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-bišče</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежбище.html>ле́жбище</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">léžbišče</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежбище.html>ле́жбища</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежбище.html>ле́жбища</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежбище.html>ле́жбищ</a></b>)

***лезть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a> (1441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лѣзти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lězti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lězti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to crawl, climb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">leztʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залезть.html>зале́зть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влезть.html>влезть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полезть.html>поле́зть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to climb (up, on to), to scramble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>leztʹ</b> na sténu</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to climb up</b> the wall</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to clamber, to crawl, to scramble (through, into, under)</li>
<li>to get (into); to thrust the hand (into)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>leztʹ</b> v vódu</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to get</b> into the water</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:драка.html>дра́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>leztʹ</b> v dráku</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to get</b> into the fight</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to thrust oneself (upon); to intrude (upon)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>ле́зь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>lezʹ</b> ko mne!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Don't touch me! / Don't intrude on me! (protest to sexual advances)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to meddle (in, with)</li>
<li>to fit (into)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ботинок.html>боти́нки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>ле́зут</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Botínki jemú ne <b>lézut</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He can't get the boots on.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fall out, to come out (of hair or fur)</li>
<li>to stick out, to be conspicuous</li>
<li>to slip out of position</li>
<li>to come on, to do something despite obstacles or objections</li>
<li>to try to climb, to try to reach a better position in life</li>
<li>to come to pieces (of cloth or leather)</li>
<li><i>used in idioms:</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вон.html>вон</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>leztʹ</b> iz kóži <a href = vnd.unilang:вон.html>von</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go all out, to bend over backwards (get out of own skin)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́вом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карман.html>карма́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>leztʹ</b> za slóvom v karmán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have a ready tongue, not to be at a loss for a word, to have a way with words (not to rummage for a word in the pocket)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>leztʹ</b> komú-libo v dúšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to worm oneself into smb.'s confidence (to get into somebody's soul)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>leztʹ</b> ne v svojó délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to poke one's nose into other people's affairs; to pry</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>хоть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>пе́тлю</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xotʹ v pétlju <b>leztʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I am at my wit's end (ready to get a noose to hang myself)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is a concrete verb. Its abstract counterpart is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лазить.html>ла́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lázitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

***лекарь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лекарь.html>ле́карь</a> (9852)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěkarь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лекарь.html>ле́карь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lékarʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лекарь.html>ле́каря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лекарь.html>ле́кари</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лекарь.html>лекаря́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лекарь.html>ле́карей</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лекарь.html>лекаре́й</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ле́карша</b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Dated.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>doctor, medico, physician (feminine form "ле́карша" is usually considered colloquial)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лектор.html>ле́ктор</a> (11510)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лектор.html>ле́ктор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">léktor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лектор.html>ле́ктора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лектор.html>ле́кторы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лектор.html>ле́кторов</a></b>)

***лелеять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лелеять.html>леле́ять</a> (15921)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lelějati</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">ле́лям</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">léljam</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">лелі́яти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lelíjaty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and possibly also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">ललति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lalati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to play</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лелеять.html>леле́ять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">leléjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to caress, to pamper
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1889</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:лев.html>Лев</a> Николаевич <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leo_Tolstoy" class="extiw" title="w:Leo Tolstoy">Lev Nikolayevich Tolstoy</a>),  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9A%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B9%D1%86%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B0_%D1%81%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0%D1%82%D0%B0_(%D0%A2%D0%BE%D0%BB%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B9)XVI" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Крейцерова соната (Толстой)">Крейцерова <a href = vnd.unilang:соната.html>сона́та</a></a></cite>, section 16 |  translated as  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Kreutzer_Sonata" class="extiw" title="w:The Kreutzer Sonata">The Kreutzer Sonata</a>”, in Larissa Volokhonsky; Richard Pevear, transl., <cite>The Death of Ivan Ilyich and Other Stories</cite>, Vintage, 2010, page 127:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведь.html>Ведь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:влечение.html>влече́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́тям</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:животный.html>живо́тная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потребность.html>потре́бность</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кормить.html>корми́ть</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лелеять.html>леле́ять</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:защищать.html>защища́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>их</a> – <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большинство.html>большинства́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщин</a>, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vedʹ vlečénije k détjam, živótnaja potrébnostʹ kormítʹ, <b>leléjatʹ</b>, zaščiščátʹ ix – bylá, kak oná i jestʹ u bolʹšinstvá žénščin, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">For the attachment to her children, the animal need to feed, <b>pamper</b>, and protect them, was the same as in the majority of women, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>to care for, to tend, to look after
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1880</b>,  Фёдор Михайлович Достоевский (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fyodor_Dostoevsky" class="extiw" title="w:Fyodor Dostoevsky">Fyodor Mikhailovich Dostoevsky</a>),  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%91%D1%80%D0%B0%D1%82%D1%8C%D1%8F_%D0%9A%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BC%D0%B0%D0%B7%D0%BE%D0%B2%D1%8B_(%D0%94%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B5%D0%B2%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%B8%D0%B9)/%D0%9A%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%B3%D0%B0_%D0%B2%D1%82%D0%BE%D1%80%D0%B0%D1%8F/I" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Братья Карамазовы (Достоевский)/Книга вторая/I"><a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>Бра́тья</a> Карамазовы</a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Brothers_Karamazov" class="extiw" title="w:The Brothers Karamazov">The Brothers Karamazov</a></cite> | , <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Brothers_Karamazov/Book_II/Chapter_1" class="extiw" title="s:The Brothers Karamazov/Book II/Chapter 1">book 2, chapter 1</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:действительно.html>действи́тельно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>хоть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>их</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:видимо.html>ви́димо</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:опытный.html>о́пытная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dejstvítelʹno, xotʹ roz tepérʹ i ne býlo, no býlo mnóžestvo rédkix i prekrásnyx osénnix cvetóv vezdé, gde tólʹko móžno býlo ix nasadítʹ. <b>Leléjala</b> ix, vídimo, ópytnaja ruká.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In fact, although now there were no roses, there was an abundance of rare and beautiful autumn flowers, wherever it was possible to plant them. They were obviously <b>cared for</b> by an experienced hand.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>to cherish, to foster
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1893</b>,  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Orlóv brezglivo otbrásyval ot sebjá žénskije trjápki, detéj, kúxnju, médnyje kastrjúli, a ja podbirál vsjó éto i bérežno <b>leléjal</b> v svoíx mečtáx, ljubíl, prosíl <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лениво.html>лени́во</a> (3994)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:ленивый.html>лени́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lenivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лѣнивꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lěnivyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěnivъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lazy, sluggish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěniti</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ivъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěniti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěnь</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěnjь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">laziness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěnъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lazy, slow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***ленивый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ленивый.html>лени́вый</a> (5541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лѣнивꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lěnivyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěnivъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lazy, sluggish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěniti</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ivъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěniti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěnь</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěnjь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">laziness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěnъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lazy, slow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лень.html>лень</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ленивый.html>лени́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lenívyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)лени́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)лени́вей</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:ленивый.html>лени́вый</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">лениве́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lazy (unwilling to work)</li></ol>
